Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-08-31 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.22.2-3 - Drop forge-macros and perform tarbal verification during %prep
2021-08-31 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.22.2-2 - Add a patch to disable use of Brainpool Elliptic Curves
2021-08-22 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.22.2-1 - New upstream release - Disable enforcing of FIPS mode for OpenSSL
2021-07-21 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-12 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_35_Mass_Rebuild
2021-01-25 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-11 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2020-11-15 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-10 - Add runtime dependency on qt5-qtquickcontrols2
2020-10-03 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-9 - Disable fipscheck in shell wrapper as it does not work in Fedora 33+
2020-09-26 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-8 - Make shell wrapper exit with the exit code of fipscheck on failure
2020-09-26 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-7 - Calculate fipshmac for config files and shell wrapper - Run fipscheck in shell wrapper before application starts
2020-09-25 Björn Esser <besser82 at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.20.2-6 - Use a python script to generate a tailored OpenSSL configuration
